***diaken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:diaken.html>diaken</a> (23198)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:diaken.html>diaken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ecclesiastical_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Ecclesiastical Latin">Ecclesiastical Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">diaconus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">διᾱ́κονος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">diā́konos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">servant, minister</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diaken.html>diaken</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diaken.html>diakenen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diakens.html>diakens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diaken.html>diakentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">diacones</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Protestantism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deacon, person involved in an ecclesiastical lay office for social affairs and charity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Roman Catholicism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deacon, male in an unordained clerical office qualified for parish work</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deken.html>deken</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">diaconie</span></li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***diamant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:diamant.html>diamant</a> (4367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:diamant.html>diamant</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:diamant.html>diamant</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">diamas</i>, variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">adamas</i>.
</p><p>The typographic use derives from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dirck_Voskens" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Dirck Voskens">Dirck Voskens</a>, who first cut it around 1700 and presumably named it by analogy with the larger <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parel.html>parel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diamant.html>diamant</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mineralogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> diamond <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">substance</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diamant.html>diamant</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diamanten.html>diamanten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diamant.html>diamantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a diamond</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> printing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The size of type between <a href = vnd.unilang:kwart.html>kwart</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cicero.html>cicero</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:parel.html>parel</a>, equivalent to English brilliant and standardized as 4 point.</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">diarrhée</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">diarrie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">diarrhoea</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">διάρροια</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">diárrhoia</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a flowing-through; diarrhea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diarree.html>diarree</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diarree.html>diarreeën</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>diarrhea
<ul><li><b>1994</b>, J.F. <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijn.html>Wijn</a>, W.<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>.J.M. Hekkens, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:fysiologie.html>Fysiologie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a></i>, Bohn Stafleu <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Loghum, page 354:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> 'burning <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a>'-syndroom <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:langdurig.html>langdurige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slechte.html>slechte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gecombineerd.html>gecombineerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> absorptiestoornissen <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:frequente.html>frequente</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:diarree.html>diarreeën</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waargenomen.html>waargenomen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krijgsgevangenen.html>krijgsgevangenen</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tropen.html>tropen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>.a. <a href = vnd.unilang:toegeschreven.html>toegeschreven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> pantotheenzuurdeficiëntie in <a href = vnd.unilang:combinatie.html>combinatie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:marginale.html>marginale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorziening.html>voorziening</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> B-vitamines.
<dl><dd>The 'burning <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a>' syndrome that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, after after continuous malnutrition combined with absorption disorders due to frequent <b>diarrheas</b>, often observed with prisoners of war in the tropics <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ascribed to, among others, deficiency in pantothenic acid combined with marginal supply of other B-vitamins.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buikloop.html>buikloop</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">buikvloed</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***dicht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a> (506)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thīht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þinhtaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tight</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dichter.html>dichter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dichtst.html>dichtst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thick, tight, dense</li>
<li>close
<dl><dd><i>„Wie <a href = vnd.unilang:vorig.html>vorig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woning.html>woning</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkocht.html>verkocht</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kreeg.html>kreeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:prijs.html>prijs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:relatief.html>relatief</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorspronkelijk.html>oorspronkelijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vraagprijs.html>vraagprijs</a> lag”, <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderzoek.html>onderzoek</a>.</i> — “Who in the previous year <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> his home, obtained a price that lay relatively <b>close</b> to the original asking price,” stated the research paper. <br /><small>(<i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ad.nl/economie/article962441.ece"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:algemeen.html>Algemeen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagblad.html>Dagblad</a></a></i>, 5 January 2007)</small></dd></dl></li>
<li>closed, shut
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> spring <a href = vnd.unilang:lachend.html>lachend</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diepe.html>diepe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> m'n <a href = vnd.unilang:ogen.html>ogen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></b>.</i> — I jump laughing into the deep with my <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> <i>shut</i>. <small> (<a href = vnd.unilang:marco.html>Marco</a> Borsato ft. Sita  |  <a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>Lopen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> Water) </small></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dichtslaan.html>dichtslaan</a> (36186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dichtslaan.html>dichtslaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slam shut, to be slammed shut</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose composure or become confused so that one becomes unable to react
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:slaat.html>slaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wanneer.html>wanneer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fauteuil.html>fauteuil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zet.html>zet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mand.html>mand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a>.</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dichtslaan.html>dichtslaan</a></b>  <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

***die.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> (23)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i>, a merger of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thē</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thia</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thiu</i> and similar forms of the demonstrative. As in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ther</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a></i> it replaced the original masculine and feminine nominative forms from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>that (masculine, feminine); <span class="use-with-mention">referring to a thing or a person further away.</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i>
<dl><dd><b>that</b> tree</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a></i>
<dl><dd><b>that</b> woman</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>those (plural); <span class="use-with-mention">referring to <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> or people further away.</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vensters.html>vensters</a></i>
<dl><dd><b>those</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>windows</a></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> who, whom, which, that
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>ken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know any people <b>who</b> can do that.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>ken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a>!</i>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, but I know somebody <b>who</b> can!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_4">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>A preceding comma may alter the meaning of a clause starting with a relative pronoun. Compare the following sentences:
</p>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>Alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:arbeiders.html>arbeiders</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:staken.html>staken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zullen.html>zullen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sancties.html>sancties</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rekenen.html>rekenen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>All workers <b>who</b> are on strike should expect sanctions.</dd></dl></li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>Alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:arbeiders.html>arbeiders</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:staken.html>staken</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zullen.html>zullen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sancties.html>sancties</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rekenen.html>rekenen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>All workers, <b>who</b> are on strike, should expect sanctions.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<p>In the first sentence, only the workers on strike are advised to expect sanctions. In the second sentence, the parenthetical phrase indicates that all the workers are on strike, and should all expect sanctions.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Aanwijzend_voornaamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:aanwijzen.html>Aanwijzend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamwoord.html>voornaamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***dief.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dief.html>dief</a> (2026)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dief.html>dief</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thiof</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þeubaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dief.html>dief</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dieven.html>dieven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diefje.html>diefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dievegge.html>dievegge</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A thief, one who <a href = vnd.unilang:steals.html>steals</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***diefstal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:diefstal.html>diefstal</a> (3783)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:diefstal.html>diefstal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">diepstale</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:diep.html>diep</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thief</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">stale</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">theft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The former part <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> the same origin as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dief.html>dief</a></i>, the latter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stāla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stēlō</i>. Replaced the Middle Dutch word <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">diefte</i>, which still survives in some dialects.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diefstal.html>diefstal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diefstallen.html>diefstallen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diefstal.html>diefstalletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>theft</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dienen.html>dienen</a> (2277)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienen.html>dienen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thienon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þewanōną</i>.

***diens.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:diens.html>diens</a> (16400)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diens.html>diens</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">demonstrative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> his, the latter's (genitive masculine and neuter singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:samen.html>Samen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Nederlander Henri Albert Gosse, <a href = vnd.unilang:jacques.html>Jacques</a> Paul <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:diens.html>diens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a> Nicolas <a href = vnd.unilang:begon.html>begon</a> Schweppe in 1790 in Zwitserland <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> mineraalwaterfabriek.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Together with the Dutch Henri Albert Gosse, <a href = vnd.unilang:jacques.html>Jacques</a> Paul and <b>the latter's</b> son Nicolas, Schweppe began a mineral water factory in 1790 in Switzerland.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">demonstrative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the latter's (genitive singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diens.html>Diens</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in a similar way as the possessive determiner <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i>. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> Dutch, but used occasionally in writing to avoid confusion. Compare:
</p>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertelde.html>vertelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a>.</i> – He <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> about his son and <b>his (own)</b> wife.</li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertelde.html>vertelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:diens.html>diens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a>.</i> – He <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> about his son and <b>the latter's</b> wife.</li></ul>
<p>The corresponding plural and feminine form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i>, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not uncommon to see "<a href = vnd.unilang:diens.html>diens</a>" used for all genders.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Aanwijzend_voornaamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:aanwijzen.html>Aanwijzend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamwoord.html>voornaamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:diens.html>diens</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><i>genitief</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kent.html>kent</a> Jakob; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:diens.html>diens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziekenhuis.html>ziekenhuis</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>

***dienst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dienst.html>dienst</a> (849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienst.html>dienst</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thionost</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þewanōstaz</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienen.html>dienen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-st</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienst.html>dienst</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diensten.html>diensten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienst.html>dienstje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>service</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dienster.html>dienster</a> (28252)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienster.html>dienster</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienster.html>diensters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienster.html>dienstertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***diep.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:diep.html>diep</a> (1064)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:diep.html>diep</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*diop</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*deupaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰewb-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">deep</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">djip</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deep</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">dyb</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">dyp</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diep.html>diep</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dieper.html>dieper</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diepst.html>diepst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deep, down low</li>
<li>profound
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diepgaand.html>diepgaand</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diepzinnig.html>diepzinnig</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***diepen.html

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:diepen.html>diepen</a></i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">diepde</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:diepte.html>diepte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">diopitha</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*diupiþō</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*deupaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diep.html>diep</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diep.html>diep</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vries.html>vries</a></i>, partial calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deep freeze</i>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vries.html>Vries</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not a noun in Dutch, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> rather <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> from the <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriezen.html>vriezen</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*deuʀ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*deuzą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰewsóm</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">demonstrative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> her, their, the latter's (genitive feminine singular and genitive plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i>).
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdachte.html>verdachte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:samen.html>samen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dochter.html>dochter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schuldig.html>schuldig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moord.html>moord</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echtgenoot.html>echtgenoot</a> [...]</i> (from a verdict of the Court of Justice at 'S-Gravenhage, 2011 <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://jure.nl/bq6330">[1]</a>)</dd>
<dd>The accused (woman) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> guilty of having murdered her husband in cooperation with a friend, her daughter and <b>the latter's</b> friend [...]</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_3">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>Dier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in a similar way as the possessive determiners <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i>. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> Dutch, but used occasionally in writing to avoid confusion. Compare:
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertelde.html>vertelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dochter.html>dochter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> of her daughter and <b>her (own)</b> husband.</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertelde.html>vertelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dochter.html>dochter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> of her daughter and <b>the latter's</b> husband.</span></div></li></ul>
<p>The corresponding masculine and neuter singular form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diens.html>diens</a></i>.
</p>

***dierbaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dierbaar.html>dierbaar</a> (9470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dierbaer</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dear, precious</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-baar</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-able, -worthy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the former a dialectal form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duur.html>duur</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dierbaar.html>dierbaar</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dierbaarder.html>dierbaarder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dierbaarst.html>dierbaarst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dear, prized by someone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> precious, of great value</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pricey</li>
<li>(<i>in devotional circles</i>) highly/morally moving, touching</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kostbaar.html>kostbaar</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duur.html>duur</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geprezen.html>geprezen</a></span></li>
<li>(pricy only) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">prijzig</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">dierbaarheid</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">allerdierbaarst</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">overdierbaar</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dierbaar.html>dierbaar</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:waaraan.html>waaraan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarde.html>waarde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hecht.html>hecht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarvan.html>waarvan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houdt.html>houdt</a>
